	culture = first_man

	19.1.1 = {
		trait = arrogant
		trait = ambitious
		trait = wrathful

}

###### HOUSE BARATHEON (id = dynn_Baratheon)

### Ours is the Fury
###Added by Chrismj89 in Colaboration with Oga

#Done the Baratheon family tree. Not the cadet branches of Bolling and Wensington yet though. Rhaelle and the Lannister patriarchs have been updated/corrected too.
# I've added charinfo and a new house 'Godsgrief' its the same CoA of Baratheon so that will be easy. Bolling and Wensington have separate CoA. They are on the wiki though.

#- House Baratheon - House Godsgrief. Founders of Bolling and Wensington. \Update/ Godsgrief now Durrandon.
#Plus connections. Targaryen and Lannister.

	trait = honorable

			add_trait_force_tooltip = bastard_founder
